Find humor every day. care about others when you feel a way then listen to someone else. Some way to not let yourself carry negative baggage around with you like armor or as a bag of weapons to use against those around you. I liked his use of Bits Games and random YouTubes to deflect negativity from news or life or online stuff get his show and its crew down. He just made a statement about it identified the situation then quickly turned it around with humor compassion or even a random commercial that could be purposefully placed that was slightly light or funny. He will always be the light that taught us how to deal with our own grief of losing all 4 parents in the 8 years of his show. The loss of Obama and introduction to the past 2 presidents that are so different from Obama its not even easy to say President at times in comparison. I will miss this show. So "Hats off waving as you fly away to UK Mr. Corden we thank you forever but know it isn't even enough times to show how much you did for our 32 year old family."
